# Congressional Career

### Summary

> * Andy Ogles was elected to Congress in 2022 after winning a crowded Republican primary for Tennessee’s newly redrawn 5th District, becoming the first Republican to represent Nashville in this seat since Reconstruction. [Tennessean](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/elections/2024/07/24/tennessee-5th-congressional-district-republican-primary-andy-ogles-courtney-johnston/74206555007/)
> 
> * During his first term, Ogles aligned with the House Freedom Caucus and was a vocal critic of the Biden administration, frequently introducing high-profile and controversial legislation, such as bills to impeach President Biden and Vice President Harris, propose a third term for Trump, and push back on progressive causes. [ProPublica](https://www.propublica.org/article/roommates-steve-berger-mike-johnson-andy-ogles-right-wing-influence-townhouse) [WSMV](https://www.wsmv.com/2025/01/24/tn-congressman-proposes-giving-president-trump-3rd-term/)
> 
> * Ogles claimed legislative productivity with over 100 bills and amendments filed during his first term; however, none of the bills he personally sponsored became law, and only a handful advanced past committee, while some amendments and co-sponsored bills were passed. [Tennessean](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/elections/2024/07/24/tennessee-5th-congressional-district-republican-primary-andy-ogles-courtney-johnston/74206555007/)
> 
> * He faced criticism and negative press for exaggerated and inconsistent biographical claims, high levels of taxpayer-funded spending on office mailers and reimbursements, and for being less responsive to constituents, with some opponents accusing him of prioritizing self-promotion and national media over district needs. [Nashville Scene](https://www.nashvillescene.com/news/coverstory/pleading-the-5th-rep-andy-ogles-stumbles-into-congress/article_f4b9e4bc-edd7-11ed-ab4b-bbed5a52185a.html), [Tennessean](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/2024/06/04/us-rep-andy-ogles-tn-spends-335k-taxpayer-funded-mailers/73837980007/)
> 
> * Ogles consistently aligned himself with hardline conservative positions, opposed House Speaker Kevin McCarthy for multiple rounds in early 2023 before eventually supporting him, and continued to participate in high-profile culture war and impeachment efforts throughout his tenure. [Nashville Post](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6CN4-3R81-DXVP-T40W-00000-00&context=1519360), [Tennessean](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/elections/2024/07/24/tennessee-5th-congressional-district-republican-primary-andy-ogles-courtney-johnston/74206555007/)
> 
> * Despite ongoing ethics scrutiny and criticism from both media and political opponents, Ogles secured re-election in 2024 with strong support from Trump and Republican voters in his district. [Nashville Post](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6DC0-W4R1-JBCN-32CG-00000-00&context=1519360), [MSNBC](https://www.msnbc.com/rachel-maddow-show/maddowblog/ethics-troubles-gops-andy-ogles-become-even-serious-rcna186362)


### Congressional Actions and Controversies

#### <span style="text-decoration: underline; border-bottom: 1px solid #999; padding-bottom: 2px;">Public Statements and Social Media Posts</span>

**August 2021: Ogles Declared The U.S. Is In A 'Cultural And Spiritual War'** According to Tennessee Star, "That is, until after the election, when he realized that we are in a cultural and spiritual war. 'We are at war and I, for one, am ready to take our country back,' Ogles declared to cheers from the attendees." [Tennessee Star, [8/2/21](https://tennesseestar.com/news/maury-county-mayor-andy-ogles-conservative-tennessee-is-a-state-of-half-measures/klbaigert/2021/08/02/)]

**2023: Andy Ogles Joined House Freedom Caucus** According to Nashville Scene, Ogles "quickly joined [Matt Gaetz, Marjorie Taylor Greene, Lauren Boebert, and Jim Jordan] in the House Freedom Caucus, the ideological successor to the Tea Party Movement of the 2010s." [Nashville Scene, [5/11/23](https://www.nashvillescene.com/news/coverstory/pleading-the-5th-rep-andy-ogles-stumbles-into-congress/article_f4b9e4bc-edd7-11ed-ab4b-bbed5a52185a.html)]

**2023: Andy Ogles Was Criticized For Exaggerated And Inconsistent Biographical Claims** According to Nashville Scene, "a string of stories from NewsChannel 5 reporter Phil Williams blew holes in his reputation at home. In the heat of a national controversy over the fabricated résumé of first-term GOP U.S. Rep. George Santos of New York, Williams found a pattern of exaggerated and inconsistent biographical details in the stories Ogles told voters during his campaign." [Nashville Scene, [5/11/23](https://www.nashvillescene.com/news/coverstory/pleading-the-5th-rep-andy-ogles-stumbles-into-congress/article_f4b9e4bc-edd7-11ed-ab4b-bbed5a52185a.html)]

**2023: Andy Ogles Was Accused Of Exaggerating And Inaccurate Resume Claims** According to Nashville Banner, "A series of revelations about Ogles’ exaggerated and inaccurate resume followed, as did mounting questions about his personal and campaign finances." [Nashville Banner, [11/5/24](https://nashvillebanner.com/2024/11/05/andy-ogles-re-election-win/)]

**Andy Ogles Was Accused Of Misrepresenting Educational And Business Credentials** According to NewsChannel 5, "NewsChannel 5 Investigates discovered that, like Santos, Ogles has misrepresented his educational and business credentials." [NewsChannel 5, [1/9/24](https://www.newschannel5.com/news/newschannel-5-investigates/revealed/revealed-tennessee-rep-andy-ogles-faces-ethics-complaint-comparison-to-george-santos)]

**2023-2024: Andy Ogles Spent $335,000 On Taxpayer-Funded Mailers And $30,000 In Reimbursements** According to Tennessean, "Ogles has spent $335,000 on taxpayer-funded mailers to tout his records, and another $30,00 in travel and expense reimbursements since taking office." [Tennessean, [7/24/24](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/2024/06/04/us-rep-andy-ogles-tn-spends-335k-taxpayer-funded-mailers/73837980007/)]

**2025: ProPublica Noted Ogles Has Faced Allegations Of Inflating His Resume** According to ProPublica, "He has faced allegations that he inflated his resume, claiming alternatively to have been an economist, a member of law enforcement and an expert on international sex trafficking, NewsChannel 5 in Nashville reported. (Ogles has acknowledged at least one mistake on his resume but said that 'my body of work speaks for itself.')" [ProPublica, [3/6/25](https://www.propublica.org/article/roommates-steve-berger-mike-johnson-andy-ogles-right-wing-influence-townhouse)]

**Ogles Faced Resume Inflation Allegations; Acknowledged At Least One Error As Of 2025** According to ProPublica, "He has faced allegations that he infated his resume, claiming alternatively to have been an economist, a member of law enforcement and an expert on international sex trafficking, NewsChannel 5 in Nashville reported. (Ogles has acknowledged at least one mistake on his resume but said that ‘my body of work speaks for itself.’)" [Tennessee Lookout, [3/6/25](https://tennesseelookout.com/2025/03/06/secretive-d-c-influence-project-appears-to-be-running-a-group-house-for-right-wing-lawmakers/)]

**Ogles Exaggerated Résumé, Congressional Behavior, And Covenant School Shooting Response Criticized By Opponents** According to Nashville Post, "His exaggerated résumé, behavior in Congress and response to the Covenant School shooting are among the reasons cited by some for continuing to oppose the incumbent." [Nashville Post, [3/18/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BKF-11C1-DXVP-T1DD-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Faced Criticism For Exaggerating His Résumé And Seeking Attention Rather Than Productivity** According to Nashville Post, "Guarente says, Ogles has fallen short by exaggerating his résumé, failing to sufficiently communicate with constituents and seeking attention rather than productivity in Washington." [Nashville Post, [3/18/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BKF-11C1-DXVP-T1DD-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Faced Criticism For Exaggerated Résumé, Congressional Behavior, And Covenant School Shooting Response** According to Nashville Post, "His exaggerated résumé, behavior in Congress and response to the Covenant School shooting are among the reasons cited by some for continuing to oppose the incumbent." [Nashville Post, [3/18/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BKH-G0H1-JBCN-32VM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Tom Guarente Criticized Ogles For Exaggerated Résumé And Lack Of Communication** According to Nashville Post, Tom Guarente says, "Specifically, Guarente says, Ogles has fallen short by exaggerating his résumé, failing to sufficiently communicate with constituents and seeking attention rather than productivity in Washington." [Nashville Post, [3/18/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BKH-G0H1-JBCN-32VM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Rush Benton Criticized Ogles's Response To Covenant Shooting And Social Media Focus** According to Nashville Post, Rush Benton says, "I just don't think it's a MAGA district, frankly. It's frustrating that we have a congressman who, it seems to me, is less about policy and more about Instagram hits or Twitter hits. He's from the camp that wants to continue to stoke the division in the country and not do anything to pull us together." [Nashville Post, [3/18/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BKH-G0H1-JBCN-32VM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023: Ledger Reported Andy Ogles Inflated His Resume** According to Ledger, Knoxville Edition, "Ogles's political liabilities before, including inflating his resume to pose as an economist with a degree in international relations who worked as a trained law enforcement officer fighting international sex crimes. None of which is what a stickler might call 'true.'" [Ledger: Knoxville Edition (Tennessee), [4/26/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BWK-WKG1-DXVP-T19V-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023-2024: Andy Ogles Was Identified As Member Of The Freedom Caucus** According to Ledger, Knoxville Edition, "Ogles is a member of the Freedom Caucus, the far-right fringe of the House who strongly oppose much government spending, unless proposed by a Republican president." [Ledger: Knoxville Edition (Tennessee), [4/26/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BWK-WKG1-DXVP-T19V-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ledger: Ogles Faced Criticism For Inflating His Resume** According to The Ledger: Nashville Edition, "I've mentioned some of Ogles's political liabilities before, including inflating his resume to pose as an economist with a degree in international relations who worked as a trained law enforcement officer fighting international sex crimes. None of which is what a stickler might call 'true.'" [Ledger: Nashville Edition, [4/26/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BWK-WKF1-DXVP-T0W2-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Used Taxpayer Funds For Digital Ads On His Legislative Record** According to Tennessean, "Freshman Tennessee U.S. Andy Ogles, R-Columbia, has used taxpayer funds to buy digital ads touting his legislative record during his first term in office." [Tennessean, [5/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BYG-YT71-JB1V-G220-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Claimed 'Records Broken' With Most Stand-Alone Legislation Passed By Any Freshman** According to Tennessean, "In his ads, Ogles says he's responsible for 'records broken' with the 'most stand-alone legislation passed by any freshman.'" [Tennessean, [5/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BYG-YT71-JB1V-G220-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles' Digital Ad Buys Approved By House Communications Standards Commission** According to Tennessean, "Congressional records indicate Ogles' ad buy was deemed expensable, or 'frankable,' by the bipartisan House Communications Standards Commission." [Tennessean, [5/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BYG-YT71-JB1V-G220-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Sought Approval For 15 Taxpayer-Funded Digital Ad Buys, Mass Emails, And Texts Since February** According to Tennessean, "Ogles has sought approval for 15 taxpayer-funded digital ad buys, mass emails and text messages since February." [...] Ogles has sought approval for 15 taxpayer-funded digital ad buys, mass emails and text messages since February." Ogles has sought approval for 15 taxpayer-funded digital ad buys, mass emails and text messages since February." [Leaf-Chronicle, [5/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BYP-XX81-DXGX-60TS-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: House Commission Approved Ogles’ Taxpayer-Funded Ad Buys** According to Columbia Daily Herald, "Congressional records indicate Ogles' ad buy was deemed expensable, or 'frankable,' by the bipartisan House Communications Standards Commission. Ogles has sought approval for 15 taxpayer-funded digital ad buys, mass emails and text messages since February." [Columbia Daily Herald, [5/7/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BYX-X3F1-JB1V-G0SD-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Federal Law Prohibited House Franked Mail Within 90 Days Of An Election** According to Columbia Daily Herald, "Federal law prohibits franked mailings by U.S. House members within 90 days of an election." [Columbia Daily Herald, [5/7/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6BYX-X3F1-JB1V-G0SD-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Faced Scrutiny for Covenant School Shooting Response and House Leadership Stances** According to Nashville Post, "In addition to his campaign finance troubles, Ogles has faced scrutiny for his response to the Covenant School shooting in his district and his flip-flopping on Republican leadership of the House." [Nashville Post, [5/24/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C3T-H9H1-DXVP-T0BR-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Received Approval For 22 Taxpayer-Funded Communications Before Blackout Period** According to Columbia Daily Herald, "Ogles sought approval this year for 22 different communications before a June 1 blackout period ahead of the Aug. 1 primary. He sent 41 in total last year." [Columbia Daily Herald, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G50S-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Stated Constituent Service As Highest Priority In New District** According to Columbia Daily Herald, "'Constituent service is the highest priority for my office and staff, and maintaining good constituent communication in a brand-new district is absolutely necessary to ensure that people know how we can help them navigate problems with federal agencies like the IRS, VA, or Social Security and how we fight for Tennessee's values in D.C.,' Ogles said in a statement in a response to an inquiry from The Tennessean." [Columbia Daily Herald, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G50S-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**December 2023: Ogles Purchased Radio Ads On Border, Cost Of Living, And Government Spending** According to Columbia Daily Herald, "In December, Ogles bought four 30-second radio ads on border issues, cost of living and rising costs of government. None of the ads solicited constituent feedback. Each end with a voiceover stating, 'Paid for by official funds authorized by the House of Representatives.'" [Columbia Daily Herald, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G50S-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Cited Constituent Communication As Enablement For Providing Services** According to Columbia Daily Herald, "In a statement, Ogles said his use of taxpayer-funded communications has enabled his staff to provide constituent services on issues like veteran pay. 'Were it not for our level of constituent communication, we might not have had the opportunity to help many wonderful Tennesseans work through some very difficult times,' Ogles said." [Columbia Daily Herald, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G50S-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Jan 2023 - Mar 2024: Leaf-Chronicle Reported Ogles Spent Over $335,000 In Taxpayer Funds On Constituent Communications** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "U.S. Rep. Andy Ogles, R-Columbia, spent more than $335,000 on taxpayer-funded constituent communications between January 2023 and March 2024, outpacing the rest of Tennessee's U.S. House delegation as he eyes a competitive Republican primary in the 5th Congressional District." [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**May 2024: Ogles Distributed District-Wide Digital Ads And Mailers Touting Legislative Record** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "In late May, Ogles flooded the district with digital ads and a glossy mail piece touting 'records broken' on legislation as a freshman lawmaker. The communication comes from what is known as the 'franking' privilege, which allows members of Congress to use taxpayer-funded budgets to send communications to constituents." [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023: Ogles Sought Approval For 22 Taxpayer-Funded Communications Before June Primary Blackout** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "Ogles sought approval this year for 22 different communications before a June 1 blackout period ahead of the Aug. 1 primary. He sent 41 in total last year." [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Stated Constituent Service Was Top Priority In New District** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "'Constituent service is the highest priority for my office and staff, and maintaining good constituent communication in a brand-new district is absolutely necessary to ensure that people know how we can help them navigate problems with federal agencies like the IRS, VA, or Social Security and how we fight for Tennessee's values in D.C.'" [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023: Ogles' Communications Included Text Surveys And Banner Ads On Conservative Issues** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "Among Ogles' communications were text surveys, such as a Davidson County poll asking for constituent priorities, and digital banner ads signaling Ogles' support for Israel, stricter border policies and other conservative tentpole issues." [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Dec 2023: Ogles Purchased Radio Ads On Border Issues And Cost Of Living, Using Official Funds** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "In December, Ogles bought four 30-second radio ads on border issues, cost of living and rising costs of government. None of the ads solicited constituent feedback. Each end with a voiceover stating, 'Paid for by official funds authorized by the House of Representatives.'" [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Claimed Constituent Communications Enabled Office To Assist Tennesseans With Federal Issues** According to Leaf-Chronicle, "In a statement, Ogles said his use of taxpayer-funded communications has enabled his staff to provide constituent services on issues like veteran pay. 'Were it not for our level of constituent communication, we might not have had the opportunity to help many wonderful Tennesseans work through some very difficult times,' Ogles said." [Leaf-Chronicle, [6/5/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C64-2DJ1-JB1V-G4XM-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023-2024: Knoxville News-Sentinel Reported Ogles Spent Over $335,000 On Taxpayer-Funded Constituent Communications** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "U.S. Rep. Andy Ogles, R-Columbia, spent more than $335,000 on taxpayer-funded constituent communications between January 2023 and March 2024, outpacing the rest of Tennessee's U.S. House delegation as he eyes a competitive Republican primary in the 5th Congressional District." [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**May 2024: Ogles Sent Digital Ads And Mailers Highlighting Legislative Record** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "In late May, Ogles flooded the district with digital ads and a glossy mail piece touting 'records broken' on legislation as a freshman lawmaker. The communication comes from what is known as the 'franking' privilege, which allows members of Congress to use taxpayer-funded budgets to send communications to constituents." [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Sought Approval For 22 Taxpayer-Funded Communications Before Primary Blackout** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "Ogles sought approval this year for 22 different communications before a June 1 blackout period ahead of the Aug. 1 primary. He sent 41 in total last year." [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Stated Constituent Service Was Top Priority For His Office** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "'Constituent service is the highest priority for my office and staff, and maintaining good constituent communication in a brand-new district is absolutely necessary to ensure that people know how we can help them navigate problems with federal agencies like the IRS, VA, or Social Security and how we fight for Tennessee's values in D.C.'" [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023-2024: Ogles' Spending On Communications Outpaced Tennessee Colleagues** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "Ogles' communications spending far outpaced his Tennessee colleagues in 2023 and the first quarter of 2024, according to House disbursement reports through March 2024, the most recent period that spending figures are available." [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**December 2023: Ogles Purchased Radio Ads On Border Issues And Cost Of Living** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "In December, Ogles bought four 30-second radio ads on border issues, cost of living and rising costs of government. None of the ads solicited constituent feedback. Each end with a voiceover stating, 'Paid for by official funds authorized by the House of Representatives.'" [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Maintained A Single District Office Covering Part Of Davidson County** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "Green is now the only Tennessee representative to staff a Nashville office, though Ogles and Rose both represent part of Davidson County. Ogles and Cohen, who represents the smallest Tennessee district in geographic size, are the only delegation members to maintain a single district office." [Knoxville News-Sentinel, [6/6/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C6B-1GF1-JB1V-G289-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2024: Ogles Cited Communications As Enabling His Office To Provide Constituent Services** According to Knoxville News-Sentinel, "In a statement, Ogles said his use of taxpayer-funded communications has enabled his staff to provide constituent services on issues like veteran pay. 'Were it not for our level of constituent communication, we might not have had the opportunity to help many wonderful Tennesseans work through some very difficult times,' Ogles said." **2023-2024: Andy Ogles Spent Over $335,000 On Taxpayer-Funded Constituent Communications** According to The Daily News Journal, "U.S. Rep. **Washington Post Reported That Andy Ogles Expensed $30,264 Under Receipt-Free Congressional Reimbursement Program In 2023** According to The Tennessean, "U.S. Rep. ### Legislative Activity

#### <span style="text-decoration: underline; border-bottom: 1px solid #999; padding-bottom: 2px;">Bills Introduced by Ogles (2023-2024)</span>

**2023-2024: Andy Ogles’ Original Sponsored Legislation Has Not Advanced From Committee** According to Tennessean, "Since then, none of his original sponsored legislation has moved out of committee, though he’s filed bills like the 'Study Abroad Act' to ship ‘pro-terrorist’ student protesters to Gaza, the 'Let Trump Speak Act' to ban judges from issuing gag orders for defendants, and the 'No Juicing Joe Act' require reporting of the president’s pharmaceutical use." [Tennessean, [7/24/24](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/elections/2024/07/24/tennessee-5th-congressional-district-republican-primary-andy-ogles-courtney-johnston/74206555007/)]

**2024: Andy Ogles Stated Filing Bills Is Important For When Trump Is Reelected** According to Tennessean, "Ogles has said it's important to file these bills, as they will start moving through Congress when former President Donald Trump is reelected." [Tennessean, [7/24/24](https://www.tennessean.com/story/news/politics/elections/2024/07/12/us-house-5th-district-republican-race-andy-ogles-courtney-johnston-make-pitch-in-marshall-county/74379934007/)]

**2025: ProPublica Stated Ogles Introduced Resolution To Amend Constitution Allowing Trump A Third Term** According to ProPublica, "He recently introduced a resolution to amend the Constitution so that Trump could serve a third term as president." [ProPublica, [3/6/25](https://www.propublica.org/article/roommates-steve-berger-mike-johnson-andy-ogles-right-wing-influence-townhouse)]

(Last week, Elon Musk posted a video of Ogles touting his impeachment efforts, set to the beat from the rap song 'Shook Ones, Pt. II.')" [ProPublica, [3/6/25](https://www.propublica.org/article/roommates-steve-berger-mike-johnson-andy-ogles-right-wing-influence-townhouse)]

**2025: Andy Ogles Proposed Constitutional Amendment For Three Presidential Terms** According to WSMV, "Congressman Andy Ogles is proposing an amendment that would allow a U.S. president to be elected for up to but no more than three terms. Ogles introduced a House Joint Resolution to amend the Constitution to allow for President Donald Trump to be elected and serve a third term." [WSMV, [1/24/25](https://www.wsmv.com/2025/01/24/tn-congressman-proposes-giving-president-trump-3rd-term/)]

**2025: Ogles Stated Constitutional Amendment Would Allow Trump A Third Term** According to WSMV, in a press release, Ogles said, "Give President Trump a third term!" and "To that end, I am proposing an amendment to the Constitution to revise the limitations imposed by the 22nd Amendment on presidential terms. This amendment would allow President Trump to serve three terms, ensuring that we can sustain the bold leadership our nation so desperately needs." [WSMV, [1/24/25](https://www.wsmv.com/2025/01/24/tn-congressman-proposes-giving-president-trump-3rd-term/)]

**2025: Ogles Introduced Bill To Support U.S. Acquisition Of Greenland** According to WSMV, "In mid-January, Ogles also introduced a bill that would direct Congress to support Trump’s push to acquire Greenland. The congressman and other Republican colleagues introduced the Make Greenland Great Again Act." [WSMV, [1/24/25](https://www.wsmv.com/2025/01/24/tn-congressman-proposes-giving-president-trump-3rd-term/)]

'I am proposing an amendment to the Constitution to revise the limitations imposed by the 22 Amendment on presidential terms.' Ogles shared." Soaring gas and groceries costs have crushed countless families' financial security. Social media platforms were coerced into censoring free speech and suppressing vital medical information. Meanwhile, servicemembers have been stripped of their pay and rank for refusing a hastily approved experimental vaccine. The list of this administration's failures is as long as it is egregious," Ogles further stated. ### Public Statements and Social Media Posts

**June 2024: Ogles Spent $335,000 On Taxpayer-Funded Constituent Communications** According to Tennessean, "U.S. Rep. Andy Ogles, R-Columbia, spent more than $335,000 on taxpayer-funded constituent communications between January 2023 and March 2024, outpacing the rest of Tennessee's U.S. House delegation as he eyes a competitive Republican primary in the 5th Congressional District." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**May 2024: Ogles Sent Mailers And Digital Ads Touting Legislative Record** According to Tennessean, "In late May, Ogles flooded the district with digital ads and a glossy mail piece touting ‘records broken’ on legislation as a freshman lawmaker. The communication comes from what is known as the ‘franking’ privilege, which allows members of Congress to use taxpayer-funded budgets to send communications to constituents." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**2023-2024: Ogles Sought Approval For 22 Communications Before Primary Blackout** According to Tennessean, "Ogles sought approval this year for 22 different communications before a June 1 blackout period ahead of the Aug. 1 primary. He sent 41 in total last year." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Prioritized Constituent Communication In New District, He Said In 2024 Statement** According to Tennessean, "'As the freshman Congressman for a brand-new district, I can tell you from firsthand experience that many people in middle Tennessee still don't know who their Congressman is ... Constituent service is the highest priority for my office and staff, and maintaining good constituent communication in a brand-new district is absolutely necessary ...' Ogles said in a statement in response to an inquiry from The Tennessean." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles' Communications Included Text Surveys And Digital Banner Ads On Conservative Issues** According to Tennessean, "Among Ogles' communications were text surveys, such as a Davidson County poll asking for constituent priorities, and digital banner ads signaling Ogles' support for Israel, stricter border policies and other conservative tentpole issues." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**December 2023: Ogles Ran Four Radio Ads On Border And Cost Issues, Not Soliciting Feedback** According to Tennessean, "In December, Ogles bought four 30-second radio ads on border issues, cost of living and rising costs of government. None of the ads solicited constituent feedback. Each end with a voiceover stating, 'Paid for by official funds authorized by the House of Representatives.'" [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Maintained Only One District Office As Of 2024, Like Rep. Cohen** According to Tennessean, "Ogles and Cohen, who represents the smallest Tennessee district in geographic size, are the only delegation members to maintain a single district office." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

**Ogles Said His Communications Enabled Staff To Provide Constituent Services** According to Tennessean, "In a statement, Ogles said his use of taxpayer-funded communications has enabled his staff to provide constituent services on issues like veteran pay. 'Were it not for our level of constituent communication, we might not have had the opportunity to help many wonderful Tennesseans work through some very difficult times,' Ogles said." [Tennessean, [6/4/24](https://advance.lexis.com/api/document?collection=news&id=urn:contentItem:6C5X-3571-JB1V-G1HY-00000-00&context=1519360)]

The communication comes from what is known as the 'franking' privilege, which allows members of Congress to use taxpayer-funded budgets to send communications to constituents."
